\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!ANOVA@{ANOVA}}
\index{ANOVA@{ANOVA}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ANOVA()}{ANOVA()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classCMBVector}{CMBVector}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+ANOVA (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{use\+\_\+log }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs one-\/way ANOVA for all elements across source groups. 

Conducts analysis of variance to test whether mean concentrations differ significantly among source groups for each element.

Null hypothesis\+: μ₁ = μ₂ = ... = μₖ (all source means equal)


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em use\+\_\+log} & If true, perform ANOVA on log-\/transformed concentrations; if false, use linear-\/space concentrations\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classCMBVector}{CMBVector} of p-\/values for each element, labeled with element names
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Lower p-\/values indicate significant differences among sources 

Target group is excluded from analysis 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_aefe0ad8c4792a3041ae20102ba8956c9}\label{classSourceSinkData_aefe0ad8c4792a3041ae20102ba8956c9} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!ANOVA@{ANOVA}}
\index{ANOVA@{ANOVA}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ANOVA()}{ANOVA()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structANOVA__info}{ANOVA\+\_\+info}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+ANOVA (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const string \&}]{element,  }\item[{bool}]{use\+\_\+log }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs one-\/way ANOVA for a single element across source groups. 

Conducts detailed analysis of variance decomposing total variance into between-\/group and within-\/group components.

ANOVA decomposition\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item SST (Total) = SSB + SSW
\item SSB (Between-\/group) = Σ n\+\_\+i(μ\+\_\+i -\/ μ\+\_\+grand)²
\item SSW (Within-\/group) = Σ Σ (x\+\_\+ij -\/ μ\+\_\+i)²
\item F-\/statistic = MSB / MSW
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em element} & Name of the element to analyze \\
\hline
{\em use\+\_\+log} & If true, perform ANOVA on log-\/transformed concentrations\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{structANOVA__info}{ANOVA\+\_\+info} structure containing SST, SSB, SSW, MSB, MSW, F, and p-\/value 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_a058848caa99cfe960d968d36bfdf6e52}\label{classSourceSinkData_a058848caa99cfe960d968d36bfdf6e52} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!AssignAllDistributions@{AssignAllDistributions}}
\index{AssignAllDistributions@{AssignAllDistributions}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AssignAllDistributions()}{AssignAllDistributions()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Assign\+All\+Distributions (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Assign distributions to all elements at both dataset and group levels. 

For each element\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item At dataset level\+: Selects best-\/fitting distribution (normal vs lognormal) and estimates parameters from all data
\item At group level\+: Assigns same distribution type and estimates parameters from group-\/specific data
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

Special handling for isotopes\+: Always uses normal distribution regardless of best-\/fit results.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Should be called after \doxylink{classSourceSinkData_ad0c6334acce4ffd543ebbdee5d1f4967}{Populate\+Element\+Distributions()} 
\end{DoxyNote}


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8cpp_source_l00557}{557}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8cpp_source}{sourcesinkdata.\+cpp}}.

\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!BetweenGroupCovarianceMatrix@{BetweenGroupCovarianceMatrix}}
\index{BetweenGroupCovarianceMatrix@{BetweenGroupCovarianceMatrix}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{BetweenGroupCovarianceMatrix()}{BetweenGroupCovarianceMatrix()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily CMatrix Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Between\+Group\+Covariance\+Matrix (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Computes between-\/group covariance matrix. 

Calculates covariance matrix based on deviations of group means from the overall mean. Represents the "{}signal"{} or between-\/group scatter.

Formula\+: S\+\_\+B = Σ\mbox{[}n\+\_\+i × (μ\+\_\+i -\/ μ\+\_\+overall)(μ\+\_\+i -\/ μ\+\_\+overall)ᵀ\mbox{]} / N

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Between-\/group covariance matrix (num\+\_\+elements × num\+\_\+elements)
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Target group excluded 
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{BootStrap()}{BootStrap()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classCMBTimeSeriesSet}{CMBTime\+Series\+Set}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Boot\+Strap (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const double \&}]{percentage,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{num\+\_\+iterations,  }\item[{string}]{target\+\_\+sample,  }\item[{bool}]{use\+\_\+softmax }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs bootstrap uncertainty analysis on source contributions. 

Conducts bootstrap resampling to estimate uncertainty in source contribution estimates. Each bootstrap iteration randomly excludes a percentage of source samples, re-\/solves the CMB model, and records the resulting contributions.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em percentage} & Percentage of source samples to exclude per iteration (0-\/100) \\
\hline
{\em num\+\_\+iterations} & Number of bootstrap iterations \\
\hline
{\em target\+\_\+sample} & Name of target sample to apportion \\
\hline
{\em use\+\_\+softmax} & If true, use softmax transformation for contributions\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classCMBTimeSeriesSet}{CMBTime\+Series\+Set} containing contribution estimates from all iterations
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Progress updates sent to rtw\+\_\+ if available 
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{BootStrap()}{BootStrap()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Boot\+Strap (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classResults}{Results}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{results,  }\item[{const double \&}]{percentage,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{num\+\_\+iterations,  }\item[{string}]{target\+\_\+sample,  }\item[{bool}]{use\+\_\+softmax }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs bootstrap analysis and generates comprehensive uncertainty results. 

Conducts bootstrap resampling with full statistical analysis including\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Time series of contribution estimates
\item Posterior distributions of contributions
\item 95\% credible intervals (2.\+5th to 97.\+5th percentiles)
\item Mean and median contribution estimates
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em results} & Pointer to \doxylink{classResults}{Results} object to populate with analysis outputs \\
\hline
{\em percentage} & Percentage of source samples to exclude per iteration (0-\/100) \\
\hline
{\em num\+\_\+iterations} & Number of bootstrap iterations \\
\hline
{\em target\+\_\+sample} & Name of target sample to apportion \\
\hline
{\em use\+\_\+softmax} & If true, use softmax transformation\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if analysis completed successfully
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Generates stacked bar chart for contributions (if iterations ≤ 100) 

Computes posterior distributions with 100 bins 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_a3ef992e7b7757f4105273849836b96f1}\label{classSourceSinkData_a3ef992e7b7757f4105273849836b96f1} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!BoxCoxTransformed@{BoxCoxTransformed}}
\index{BoxCoxTransformed@{BoxCoxTransformed}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{BoxCoxTransformed()}{BoxCoxTransformed()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classSourceSinkData}{Source\+Sink\+Data}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Box\+Cox\+Transformed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{calculate\+\_\+optimal\+\_\+lambda = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Applies Box-\/\+Cox transformation to all source groups for normalization. 

Transforms elemental concentrations using the Box-\/\+Cox power transformation to improve normality of distributions. This is useful for statistical analyses that assume normally distributed data (e.\+g., t-\/tests, ANOVA, discriminant analysis).

Box-\/\+Cox transformation\+: y = (x\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}λ -\/ 1) / λ (or ln(x) if λ = 0)

The optimal λ parameter for each element is determined by maximum likelihood estimation to best achieve normality.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em calculate\+\_\+optimal\+\_\+lambda} & If true, compute optimal λ for each element; if false, use default transformation\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
New \doxylink{classSourceSinkData}{Source\+Sink\+Data} object with transformed concentrations
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Target group is not transformed (only sources) 

Element distributions are recalculated after transformation 

Original data is preserved (returns new object)
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{classSourceSinkData_a31fcf5281c4834fdf930e7960f8bd438}{Optimal\+Box\+Cox\+Parameters()} for λ \doxylink{classSourceSinkData_a699b39191b623657dba4ae384105f5a7}{parameter} computation 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{BracketTest()}{BracketTest()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classCMBMatrix}{CMBMatrix}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Bracket\+Test (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{correct\+\_\+based\+\_\+on\+\_\+om\+\_\+n\+\_\+size,  }\item[{bool}]{exclude\+\_\+elements,  }\item[{bool}]{exclude\+\_\+samples }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs bracket test on all target samples. 

Applies the bracket test to every sample in the target group, producing a matrix showing which elements in which samples fall outside source concentration ranges.

Matrix structure\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Rows\+: Elements
\item Columns\+: Target samples
\item Values\+: 0 = pass (within range), 1 = fail (outside range)
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em correct\+\_\+based\+\_\+on\+\_\+om\+\_\+n\+\_\+size} & If true, apply OM/size corrections before testing \\
\hline
{\em exclude\+\_\+elements} & If true, filter out elements marked for exclusion \\
\hline
{\em exclude\+\_\+samples} & If true, filter out samples marked for exclusion\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classCMBMatrix}{CMBMatrix} of bracket test results for all target samples
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Each target sample is tested independently 

Matrix dimensions\+: (num\+\_\+elements × num\+\_\+target\+\_\+samples) 
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!BracketTest@{BracketTest}}
\index{BracketTest@{BracketTest}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{BracketTest()}{BracketTest()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classCMBVector}{CMBVector}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Bracket\+Test (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const string \&}]{target\+\_\+sample,  }\item[{bool}]{correct\+\_\+based\+\_\+on\+\_\+om\+\_\+n\+\_\+size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs bracket test to check if target concentrations fall within source ranges. 

Tests whether each element\textquotesingle{}s concentration in the target sample falls within the range (min to max) observed across all source samples. Elements outside source ranges indicate potential issues\+: missing sources, measurement errors, or non-\/conservative behavior.

Test criteria for each element\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Pass (0)\+: Target concentration within \mbox{[}min\+\_\+sources, max\+\_\+sources\mbox{]}
\item Fail (1)\+: Target concentration outside source ranges
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em target\+\_\+sample} & Name of the target sample to test \\
\hline
{\em correct\+\_\+based\+\_\+on\+\_\+om\+\_\+n\+\_\+size} & If true, apply OM/size corrections before testing\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classCMBVector}{CMBVector} of pass/fail flags (0 = pass, 1 = fail) for each element
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Flags are labeled with element names 

Failed elements are documented in target sample notes 

Test assumes conservative mixing (no gains/losses) 
\end{DoxyNote}


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8cpp_source_l02994}{2994}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8cpp_source}{sourcesinkdata.\+cpp}}.

Builds the source mean concentration matrix for isotopes. 

Constructs a matrix where each entry \mbox{[}i,j\mbox{]} represents the mean absolute concentration of isotope i in source j. Converts from delta notation to absolute concentrations.

Conversion formula\+: \mbox{[}isotope\mbox{]} = (δ/1000 + 1) × R\+\_\+standard × \mbox{[}base\+\_\+element\mbox{]}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em param\+\_\+mode} & Controls whether to use parametric or empirical means \\

\end{DoxyParams}

Matrix of size (num\+\_\+isotopes × num\+\_\+sources)
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Mixing occurs in concentration space, not delta space 
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CreateCorrectedAndFilteredDataset()}{CreateCorrectedAndFilteredDataset()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classSourceSinkData}{Source\+Sink\+Data}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Create\+Corrected\+And\+Filtered\+Dataset (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{exclude\+\_\+samples,  }\item[{bool}]{exclude\+\_\+elements,  }\item[{bool}]{omnsizecorrect,  }\item[{const string \&}]{target = {\ttfamily "{}"{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}



Create a corrected and filtered copy of the dataset. 

Creates a new \doxylink{classSourceSinkData}{Source\+Sink\+Data} object with optional filtering and corrections\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Can exclude samples not marked for analysis
\item Can exclude elements not marked for analysis
\item Can apply organic matter and particle size corrections
\item Target group is never corrected (only source groups)
\end{DoxyItemize}

This is the main method for preparing data before analysis, allowing fine control over which samples/elements to include and whether to apply normalizations.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em exclude\+\_\+samples} & If true, exclude samples not marked for analysis \\
\hline
{\em exclude\+\_\+elements} & If true, exclude elements not marked for analysis \\
\hline
{\em omnsizecorrect} & If true, apply OM and particle size corrections to sources \\
\hline
{\em target} & Target sample name (empty to use current selected\+\_\+target\+\_\+sample\+\_\+) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
New corrected and filtered \doxylink{classSourceSinkData}{Source\+Sink\+Data} object 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classSourceSinkData}{Source\+Sink\+Data}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Create\+Corrected\+Dataset (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const string \&}]{target,  }\item[{bool}]{omnsizecorrect,  }\item[{map$<$ string, \mbox{\hyperlink{structelement__information}{element\+\_\+information}} $>$ \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{elementinfo }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Create a corrected copy of the dataset for a specific target sample. 

Creates a new \doxylink{classSourceSinkData}{Source\+Sink\+Data} object with\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Only samples marked for inclusion in analysis
\item Optional organic matter and particle size corrections applied
\item Element information filtered based on analysis flags
\item All distributions populated and assigned
\end{DoxyItemize}

This method is typically used to prepare data for source apportionment of a specific target sample.

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

New \doxylink{classSourceSinkData}{Source\+Sink\+Data} object ready for analysis 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classCMBVector}{CMBVector}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+DFA\+\_\+eigvector (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Computes the primary discriminant function eigenvector. 

Calculates the eigenvector corresponding to the largest eigenvalue of S\+\_\+\+W⁻¹ × S\+\_\+B, which defines the discriminant function axis.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classCMBVector}{CMBVector} containing discriminant function coefficients
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Returns empty vector if S\+\_\+W is singular 

Uses largest eigenvalue by absolute value 
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{DFA\_P\_Value@{DFA\_P\_Value}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{DFA\_P\_Value()}{DFA\_P\_Value()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily double Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+DFA\+\_\+\+P\+\_\+\+Value (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Computes p-\/value for discriminant function analysis. 

Tests the null hypothesis that all source groups have the same mean elemental composition using Wilks\textquotesingle{} Lambda transformed to chi-\/squared.

Chi-\/squared transformation\+: χ² = -\/\mbox{[}N -\/ 1 -\/ (p + k)/2\mbox{]} × ln(Λ)

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
P-\/value for test of group equality
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
P-\/value \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 0.\+05 indicates significant differences 
\end{DoxyNote}


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8cpp_source_l04568}{4568}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8cpp_source}{sourcesinkdata.\+cpp}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{DifferentiationPower()}{DifferentiationPower()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classElemental__Profile__Set}{Elemental\+\_\+\+Profile\+\_\+\+Set}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Differentiation\+Power (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{use\+\_\+log,  }\item[{bool}]{include\+\_\+target }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes differentiation power for all source pairs. 

Performs pairwise differentiation power analysis for all combinations of source groups, generating a comprehensive matrix of source separability.

Formula\+: D = 2 × \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}μ₁ -\/ μ₂\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} / (σ₁ + σ₂)

Interpretation\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item D \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 2\+: Strong differentiation
\item D ≈ 1\+: Moderate differentiation
\item D \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 0.\+5\+: Weak differentiation
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em use\+\_\+log} & If true, compute using log-\/space statistics; if false, use linear-\/space statistics \\
\hline
{\em include\+\_\+target} & If true, include target group in comparisons\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classElemental__Profile__Set}{Elemental\+\_\+\+Profile\+\_\+\+Set} with differentiation profiles for each source pair 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_a424843f8e0b3b303b201bd6995240197}\label{classSourceSinkData_a424843f8e0b3b303b201bd6995240197} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!DifferentiationPower@{DifferentiationPower}}
\index{DifferentiationPower@{DifferentiationPower}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{DifferentiationPower()}{DifferentiationPower()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classElemental__Profile}{Elemental\+\_\+\+Profile}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Differentiation\+Power (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const string \&}]{source1,  }\item[{const string \&}]{source2,  }\item[{bool}]{use\+\_\+log }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes differentiation power metric between two sources. 

Calculates a standardized measure of how well each element differentiates between two sources. The metric quantifies separation in units of pooled standard deviations.

Formula\+: D = 2 × \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}μ₁ -\/ μ₂\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} / (σ₁ + σ₂)

Interpretation\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item D \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 2\+: Strong differentiation (means differ by \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}1 pooled std dev)
\item D ≈ 1\+: Moderate differentiation
\item D \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 0.\+5\+: Weak differentiation (substantial overlap)
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em source1} & Name of first source group \\
\hline
{\em source2} & Name of second source group \\
\hline
{\em use\+\_\+log} & If true, compute using log-\/space statistics; if false, use linear-\/space statistics\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classElemental__Profile}{Elemental\+\_\+\+Profile} containing differentiation power for each element
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Higher values indicate better discrimination ability 

Complementary to p-\/values (considers effect size, not just significance)
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_afd001b852df4d2164085ec05733ad19c}\label{classSourceSinkData_afd001b852df4d2164085ec05733ad19c} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!DifferentiationPower\_Percentage@{DifferentiationPower\_Percentage}}
\index{DifferentiationPower\_Percentage@{DifferentiationPower\_Percentage}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{DifferentiationPower\_Percentage()}{DifferentiationPower\_Percentage()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classElemental__Profile}{Elemental\+\_\+\+Profile}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Differentiation\+Power\+\_\+\+Percentage (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const string \&}]{source1,  }\item[{const string \&}]{source2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes rank-\/based differentiation percentage between two sources. 

Calculates the percentage of samples that can be correctly classified based on element concentrations using a rank-\/based approach. Provides a distribution-\/free measure of source separability.

Method\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Pool samples from both sources
\item Rank all concentrations for each element
\item Count correct classifications (Source1 samples with low ranks + Source2 samples with high ranks, or vice versa)
\item Return classification success percentage
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em source1} & Name of first source group \\
\hline
{\em source2} & Name of second source group\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classElemental__Profile}{Elemental\+\_\+\+Profile} containing classification percentages (0-\/1) for each element
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Values near 1.\+0 indicate excellent separation 

Values near 0.\+5 indicate no separation (random classification) 

Non-\/parametric (no distributional assumptions)
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{classSourceSinkData_a224aa0bcecbe077d041e54ce84437b10}{Differentiation\+Power\+\_\+\+Percentage(bool)} for all pairwise comparisons 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_a86c761dcdfb70f7c4b0403277039f3f4}\label{classSourceSinkData_a86c761dcdfb70f7c4b0403277039f3f4} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!DiscriminantFunctionAnalysis@{DiscriminantFunctionAnalysis}}
\index{DiscriminantFunctionAnalysis@{DiscriminantFunctionAnalysis}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{DiscriminantFunctionAnalysis()}{DiscriminantFunctionAnalysis()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structDFA__result}{DFA\+\_\+result}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Discriminant\+Function\+Analysis (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs discriminant function analysis for all source groups. 

Conducts pairwise discriminant function analysis (DFA) comparing each source group against all others combined. DFA identifies the linear combination of elemental concentrations that best separates each source from the rest, which helps assess source uniqueness and potential confounding.

For each source, computes\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Wilks\textquotesingle{} Lambda (measure of group separation)
\item F-\/test p-\/value (significance of separation)
\item Discriminant p-\/value (multivariate normality test)
\item Eigenvector (discriminant function coefficients)
\item Projected samples (scores along discriminant axis)
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{structDFA__result}{DFA\+\_\+result} containing statistics and projections for all sources
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Target group is excluded from analysis 

Each source is compared against all others combined ("{}one vs rest"{}) 

Lower Wilks\textquotesingle{} Lambda indicates better separation 
\end{DoxyNote}


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8cpp_source_l02814}{2814}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8cpp_source}{sourcesinkdata.\+cpp}}.

Extracts concentration distributions for all elements across sources. 

Collects all concentration values for each element across all source samples (excluding target) into \doxylink{classConcentrationSet}{Concentration\+Set} objects. This aggregates data for statistical analysis of elemental distributions across the entire source dataset.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Map of element names to \doxylink{classConcentrationSet}{Concentration\+Set} objects containing all source sample concentrations for that element
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Target group samples are excluded 

Each \doxylink{classConcentrationSet}{Concentration\+Set} contains values from all sources combined 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_a2293066f6e29dfe77a4afd307dc013e9}\label{classSourceSinkData_a2293066f6e29dfe77a4afd307dc013e9} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!GetContributionVector@{GetContributionVector}}
\index{GetContributionVector@{GetContributionVector}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetContributionVector()}{GetContributionVector()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily CVector Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Get\+Contribution\+Vector (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{include\+\_\+all = {\ttfamily true} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Retrieves the current source contribution fractions. 

Returns a vector of contribution fractions from each source. Contributions represent the fraction of the target sample originating from each source, subject to the constraint\+: Σ f\+\_\+i = 1.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em include\+\_\+all} & If true, returns all n contributions including the constrained one. If false, returns only the n-\/1 independent contributions used in optimization. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Vector of contribution fractions, size n or n-\/1
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
All contributions satisfy\+: 0 ≤ f\+\_\+i ≤ 1 and Σ f\+\_\+i = 1 
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{GetContributionVectorSoftmax@{GetContributionVectorSoftmax}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetContributionVectorSoftmax()}{GetContributionVectorSoftmax()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily CVector Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Get\+Contribution\+Vector\+Softmax (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Retrieves the softmax parameters for source contributions. 

Returns the unconstrained softmax parameters x\+\_\+i that are transformed to contribution fractions via\+: f\+\_\+i = exp(x\+\_\+i) / Σ exp(x\+\_\+j)

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Vector of softmax parameters, size n (all sources)
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Softmax parameters are unbounded\+: x\+\_\+i ∈ (-\/∞, +∞) 
\end{DoxyNote}

Finds and retrieves an elemental profile by sample name. 

Searches all groups (sources and target) for a sample with the given name and returns a pointer to its elemental profile. Useful when the group containing the sample is unknown.

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Pointer to the elemental profile if found, nullptr otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Searches all groups sequentially until sample is found 

Returns pointer to internal data -\/ do not delete 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classResultItem}{Result\+Item}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Get\+Estimated\+Element\+Mean (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes actual mean concentrations from estimated log-\/normal parameters. 

Calculates the actual concentration means for each element in each source using the estimated μ and σ parameters from Bayesian inference.

Formula\+: Mean = exp(μ + σ²/2)

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classResultItem}{Result\+Item} containing \doxylink{classElemental__Profile__Set}{Elemental\+\_\+\+Profile\+\_\+\+Set} with mean concentrations 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetEstimatedElementMu()}{GetEstimatedElementMu()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classResultItem}{Result\+Item}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Get\+Estimated\+Element\+Mu (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Retrieves estimated μ parameters from Bayesian inference for source elements. 

Returns the inferred μ (log-\/space mean) parameters for each element in each source group as estimated during MCMC sampling or optimization.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classResultItem}{Result\+Item} containing \doxylink{classElemental__Profile__Set}{Elemental\+\_\+\+Profile\+\_\+\+Set} with inferred μ values
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Uses Get\+Estimated\+Mu() -\/ updated during MCMC/optimization 
\end{DoxyNote}

Retrieves estimated σ parameters from Bayesian inference for source elements.

\end{DoxyNote}

Get the fitted distribution for a specific element at dataset level. 

Returns a pointer to the \doxylink{classDistribution}{Distribution} object fitted to all data for this element (across all groups). This is the distribution used for likelihood calculations in MCMC.

\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!GetMLRResults@{GetMLRResults}}
\index{GetMLRResults@{GetMLRResults}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetMLRResults()}{GetMLRResults()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classResultItem}{Result\+Item}} $>$ Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Get\+MLRResults (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Retrieves multiple linear regression results for all sample groups. 

Collects the organic matter (OM) and particle size regression models for each source group. These regressions are used to correct elemental concentrations for variations in OM content and particle size distribution.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Vector of Result\+Items, one per sample group, containing MLR models
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Each \doxylink{classResultItem}{Result\+Item} is configured for table display 

Includes both source groups and target group 

Regressions must be computed first via \doxylink{classSourceSinkData_a146eb84093b492d9674b6eaed24eec47}{Perform\+Regression\+Vs\+OMAnd\+Size()} 
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{GetObjectiveFunctionValue@{GetObjectiveFunctionValue}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetObjectiveFunctionValue()}{GetObjectiveFunctionValue()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily double Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Get\+Objective\+Function\+Value (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns the objective function value for optimization algorithms. 

Computes the negative log-\/likelihood based on the current parameter values and estimation mode. Used by optimization algorithms where minimizing -\/\doxylink{generalplotter_8h_a59a611294e28b1fc7fe031295c99895dadc1d71bbb5c4d2a5e936db79ef10c19f}{log(\+L)} is equivalent to maximizing likelihood L.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Negative log-\/likelihood value (lower values indicate better fit) 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Retrieves the contributions from all sources.

\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The last element is computed as (1 -\/ sum of other contributions) 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_a6e3cabf9a8b003d42658aaf9252bb6c3}\label{classSourceSinkData_a6e3cabf9a8b003d42658aaf9252bb6c3} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!Gradient@{Gradient}}
\index{Gradient@{Gradient}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Gradient()}{Gradient()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily CVector Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Gradient (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const CVector \&}]{parameters,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8h_a7217c3f8d8d82605548bded13f396d2a}{estimation\+\_\+mode}}}]{est\+\_\+mode }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Computes the normalized gradient of the log-\/likelihood function. 

Calculates the gradient vector ∇log(\+L) using numerical differentiation (finite differences). The gradient points in the direction of steepest ascent for the log-\/likelihood.

Numerical Differentiation\+: ∂log(\+L)/∂θ\+\_\+i ≈ \mbox{[}log(L(θ + ε·e\+\_\+i)) -\/ log(L(θ))\mbox{]} / ε


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em parameters} & \doxylink{classParameter}{Parameter} vector at which to evaluate the gradient \\
\hline
{\em est\+\_\+mode} & Estimation mode determining which likelihood components to include \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Normalized gradient vector (unit length\+: \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}∇log(L)\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} = 1)
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The gradient is normalized by its L2 norm for numerical stability 
\end{DoxyNote}

Referenced by \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8cpp_source_l01993}{Gradient\+Update()}}.

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_aa749b603f847f91cbb8465f73b686332}\label{classSourceSinkData_aa749b603f847f91cbb8465f73b686332} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!GradientUpdate@{GradientUpdate}}
\index{GradientUpdate@{GradientUpdate}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GradientUpdate()}{GradientUpdate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily CVector Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Gradient\+Update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8h_a7217c3f8d8d82605548bded13f396d2a}{estimation\+\_\+mode}}}]{estmode = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8h_a7217c3f8d8d82605548bded13f396d2aa1758518884935ab40d1191e04ff0cdd3}{estimation\+\_\+mode\+::elemental\+\_\+profile\+\_\+and\+\_\+contribution}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs one gradient ascent step with adaptive step size. 

Executes a single iteration of gradient ascent optimization on the log-\/likelihood function using an adaptive step size (distance\+\_\+coeff\+\_\+).

Algorithm\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Compute gradient direction at current parameters
\item Try step sizes\+: distance\+\_\+coeff\+\_\+ and 2×distance\+\_\+coeff\+\_\+
\item Accept step that improves likelihood
\item Adjust step size for next iteration
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em estmode} & Estimation mode determining which likelihood components to include \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Updated parameter vector after the gradient step
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Modifies distance\+\_\+coeff\+\_\+ member variable for next iteration 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily double Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Grand\+Mean (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const string \&}]{element,  }\item[{bool}]{use\+\_\+log }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Computes grand mean concentration for an element across all sources. 

Calculates the overall mean concentration weighted by sample sizes across all source groups (excluding target).

Formula\+: μ\+\_\+grand = Σ(n\+\_\+i × μ\+\_\+i) / Σ(n\+\_\+i)


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em element} & Name of the element \\
\hline
{\em use\+\_\+log} & If true, compute using log-\/space means \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Weighted grand mean concentration
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Target group is excluded 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Initialize\+Contributions\+Randomly (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Initialize source contributions randomly (linear constraint) 

Randomly initializes contribution values for all sources such that they sum to 1.\+0 and all values are non-\/negative. Uses uniform random sampling with rejection until valid contributions are found.

Always returns true

\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!InitializeContributionsRandomlySoftmax@{InitializeContributionsRandomlySoftmax}}
\index{InitializeContributionsRandomlySoftmax@{InitializeContributionsRandomlySoftmax}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{InitializeContributionsRandomlySoftmax()}{InitializeContributionsRandomlySoftmax()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Initialize\+Contributions\+Randomly\+Softmax (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Initialize source contributions randomly (softmax transformation) 

Randomly initializes contribution values using softmax transformation of normally distributed random variables. This ensures contributions automatically sum to 1.\+0 and are non-\/negative without rejection sampling.

Softmax transformation\+: contribution\+\_\+i = exp(\+X\+\_\+i) / sum(exp(\+X\+\_\+j)) where X \texorpdfstring{$\sim$}{\string~} N(0,1)

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Always returns true 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Initialize\+Parameters\+And\+Observations (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const string \&}]{targetsamplename,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8h_a7217c3f8d8d82605548bded13f396d2a}{estimation\+\_\+mode}}}]{est\+\_\+mode = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8h_a7217c3f8d8d82605548bded13f396d2aa1758518884935ab40d1191e04ff0cdd3}{estimation\+\_\+mode\+::elemental\+\_\+profile\+\_\+and\+\_\+contribution}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initialize parameters and observations for MCMC optimization. 

Sets up the complete parameter space and observation vector for Bayesian inference of source contributions and/or source profiles. The exact parameters created depend on the estimation mode\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item only\+\_\+contributions\+: Only source contribution parameters
\item elemental\+\_\+profile\+\_\+and\+\_\+contribution\+: Contributions + mu/sigma for each source-\/element
\item source\+\_\+elemental\+\_\+profiles\+\_\+based\+\_\+on\+\_\+source\+\_\+data\+: Only source profile parameters
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em targetsamplename} & Name of the target sample to unmix \\
\hline
{\em est\+\_\+mode} & Estimation mode controlling which parameters to optimize \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if successful, false if data not loaded
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Must be called before running MCMC or optimization 
\end{DoxyNote}

Calculates the total log-\/likelihood for Bayesian source apportionment. 

Computes the posterior log-\/likelihood by summing multiple components based on the estimation mode. Components include source data likelihood, observation likelihood (elements and isotopes), and contribution priors.

Calculates the log-\/likelihood of the model prediction versus measured data. 

Compares the model\textquotesingle{}s predicted elemental concentrations against the observed data for the selected target sample. Computed in log-\/space assuming log-\/normally distributed errors.

Formula\+: \doxylink{generalplotter_8h_a59a611294e28b1fc7fe031295c99895dadc1d71bbb5c4d2a5e936db79ef10c19f}{log(\+L)} = -\/n\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}log(σ) -\/ \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}log(C\+\_\+pred) -\/ \doxylink{generalplotter_8h_a59a611294e28b1fc7fe031295c99895dadc1d71bbb5c4d2a5e936db79ef10c19f}{log(\+C\+\_\+obs)}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}² / (2σ²)


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em est\+\_\+mode} & Estimation mode determining how predictions are made \\
\hline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily double Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Log\+Likelihood\+Modelvs\+Measured\+\_\+\+Isotope (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8h_a7217c3f8d8d82605548bded13f396d2a}{estimation\+\_\+mode}}}]{est\+\_\+mode = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8h_a7217c3f8d8d82605548bded13f396d2aa1758518884935ab40d1191e04ff0cdd3}{estimation\+\_\+mode\+::elemental\+\_\+profile\+\_\+and\+\_\+contribution}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Calculates the log-\/likelihood of model versus measured isotopic data. 

Compares the model\textquotesingle{}s predicted isotopic delta values against the observed isotopic data for the selected target sample. Operates in linear space assuming normally distributed errors in delta values.

Formula\+: \doxylink{generalplotter_8h_a59a611294e28b1fc7fe031295c99895dadc1d71bbb5c4d2a5e936db79ef10c19f}{log(\+L)} = -\/n\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}log(σ\+\_\+iso) -\/ \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}δ\+\_\+pred -\/ δ\+\_\+obs\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}² / (2σ\+\_\+iso²)


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em est\+\_\+mode} & Estimation mode determining how predictions are made \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Log-\/likelihood value 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Calculates the log prior probability for source contributions. 

Evaluates whether the current source contributions are physically valid by checking if all contributions are non-\/negative. Acts as a constraint in Bayesian inference.

-\/1e10 if any contribution is negative, 0 if all valid

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MCMC()}{MCMC()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classResults}{Results}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+MCMC (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const string \&}]{target\+\_\+sample,  }\item[{map$<$ string, string $>$}]{arguments,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classCMCMC}{CMCMC}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classSourceSinkData}{Source\+Sink\+Data}} $>$ \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{mcmc,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classProgressWindow}{Progress\+Window}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{progress\+\_\+window,  }\item[{const string \&}]{working\+\_\+folder }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs Markov Chain Monte Carlo analysis for Bayesian source apportionment. 

Conducts full Bayesian inference using MCMC sampling to estimate posterior distributions of source contributions and model parameters. Generates comprehensive uncertainty quantification including credible intervals, posterior distributions, and predicted concentrations.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em target\+\_\+sample} & Name of target sample to apportion \\
\hline
{\em arguments} & Map of MCMC settings (number of samples, chains, burnin, etc.) \\
\hline
{\em mcmc} & Pointer to MCMC sampler object \\
\hline
{\em progress\+\_\+window} & Pointer to progress window for updates \\
\hline
{\em working\+\_\+folder} & Base directory for output files\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classResults}{Results} object containing all MCMC outputs and credible intervals
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Burnin samples excluded from posterior statistics 

Last contribution computed from sum constraint 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classCMBMatrix}{CMBMatrix}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+MCMC\+\_\+\+Batch (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{map$<$ string, string $>$}]{arguments,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classCMCMC}{CMCMC}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classSourceSinkData}{Source\+Sink\+Data}} $>$ \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{mcmc,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classProgressWindow}{Progress\+Window}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{progress\+\_\+window,  }\item[{const string \&}]{working\+\_\+folder }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs batch MCMC analysis on all target samples. 

Conducts full Bayesian MCMC analysis for every sample in the target group, generating comprehensive results for each sample and summarizing credible intervals in a matrix.

Output matrix structure\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Rows\+: Target samples
\item Columns (4 per source)\+: \mbox{[}source\mbox{]}\+\_\+low, \mbox{[}source\mbox{]}\+\_\+high, \mbox{[}source\mbox{]}\+\_\+median, \mbox{[}source\mbox{]}\+\_\+mean
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em arguments} & Map of MCMC settings \\
\hline
{\em mcmc} & Pointer to MCMC sampler object \\
\hline
{\em progress\+\_\+window} & Pointer to progress window for updates \\
\hline
{\em working\+\_\+folder} & Base directory for output folders\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classCMBMatrix}{CMBMatrix} containing credible interval statistics for all samples
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Creates subdirectory for each target sample 

All Result\+Items saved as text files 
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MeanElementalContent()}{MeanElementalContent()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classCMBVector}{CMBVector}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Mean\+Elemental\+Content (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Computes weighted mean elemental concentrations across all sources. 

Calculates the overall mean concentration for each element, weighted by the number of samples in each source group.

Formula\+: μ\+\_\+overall = Σ(n\+\_\+i × μ\+\_\+i) / Σ(n\+\_\+i)

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classCMBVector}{CMBVector} of weighted mean concentrations, labeled with element names
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Target group excluded 

Weighting ensures larger groups have proportional influence 
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{NegativeValueCheck()}{NegativeValueCheck()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily vector$<$ string $>$ Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Negative\+Value\+Check (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Checks for zero or negative concentration values across all sources. 

Scans all source groups for elements with zero or negative concentrations, which are problematic for log-\/normal distributions and certain statistical analyses. Returns detailed error messages identifying problematic elements and their source groups.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Vector of error messages describing zero/negative values found
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Returns empty vector if no issues found 

Only checks source groups (target excluded) 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_a3f4afdfad5347db1c17c01149f5d4ef7}\label{classSourceSinkData_a3f4afdfad5347db1c17c01149f5d4ef7} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!OneStepLevenberg\_Marquardt@{OneStepLevenberg\_Marquardt}}
\index{OneStepLevenberg\_Marquardt@{OneStepLevenberg\_Marquardt}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{OneStepLevenberg\_Marquardt()}{OneStepLevenberg\_Marquardt()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily CVector Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+One\+Step\+Levenberg\+\_\+\+Marquardt (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{lambda }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Performs one iteration of the Levenberg-\/\+Marquardt optimization algorithm. 

Computes the parameter update step for source contributions using the Levenberg-\/\+Marquardt algorithm, which interpolates between Gauss-\/\+Newton and gradient descent methods.

The algorithm solves\+: (J\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}T J + λ diag(\+J\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}\+T J)) dx = -\/J\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}T r


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em lambda} & Damping parameter controlling trade-\/off (typical\+: 0.\+001 to 1000) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
CVector parameter update vector dx of size (n-\/1)
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Uses standard contribution parameterization (last source implicit) 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_a31fcf5281c4834fdf930e7960f8bd438}\label{classSourceSinkData_a31fcf5281c4834fdf930e7960f8bd438} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!OptimalBoxCoxParameters@{OptimalBoxCoxParameters}}
\index{OptimalBoxCoxParameters@{OptimalBoxCoxParameters}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{OptimalBoxCoxParameters()}{OptimalBoxCoxParameters()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classCMBVector}{CMBVector}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Optimal\+Box\+Cox\+Parameters (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Computes optimal Box-\/\+Cox transformation parameters for all elements. 

Determines the optimal λ (lambda) parameter for each element\textquotesingle{}s Box-\/\+Cox transformation by maximizing the log-\/likelihood of achieving normality.

Box-\/\+Cox transformation\+: y = (x\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}λ -\/ 1) / λ (or ln(x) if λ = 0)

Special cases\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item λ = 1\+: No transformation (linear)
\item λ = 0.\+5\+: Square root transformation
\item λ = 0\+: Log transformation
\item λ = -\/1\+: Reciprocal transformation
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classCMBVector}{CMBVector} of optimal λ parameters, labeled with element names
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Search range\+: λ ∈ \mbox{[}-\/5, 5\mbox{]} 

Optimization iterations\+: 10 
\end{DoxyNote}


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8cpp_source_l03183}{3183}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8cpp_source}{sourcesinkdata.\+cpp}}.

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_a325a438ff94e4c66eade5d9e56fa6a1e}\label{classSourceSinkData_a325a438ff94e4c66eade5d9e56fa6a1e} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!OutlierAnalysisForAll@{OutlierAnalysisForAll}}
\index{OutlierAnalysisForAll@{OutlierAnalysisForAll}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{OutlierAnalysisForAll()}{OutlierAnalysisForAll()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Outlier\+Analysis\+For\+All (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const double \&}]{lower\+\_\+threshold = {\ttfamily -\/3},  }\item[{const double \&}]{upper\+\_\+threshold = {\ttfamily 3} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs outlier detection on all source groups. 

Applies Box-\/\+Cox transformation and identifies outliers based on standardized residuals. Samples with standardized values outside the threshold range are flagged as outliers in their notes.

Detection method\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Box-\/\+Cox transform each element\textquotesingle{}s distribution
\item Calculate z-\/scores\+: z = (x\+\_\+transformed -\/ μ) / σ
\item Flag outliers\+: z \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} lower\+\_\+threshold OR z \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} upper\+\_\+threshold
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em lower\+\_\+threshold} & Lower bound for standardized values (e.\+g., -\/3.\+0) \\
\hline
{\em upper\+\_\+threshold} & Upper bound for standardized values (e.\+g., +3.\+0)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Only analyzes source groups (target group excluded) 

Outliers are flagged in sample notes, not removed 

Uses Box-\/\+Cox transformation for normalization 
\end{DoxyNote}


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8cpp_source_l02801}{2801}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8cpp_source}{sourcesinkdata.\+cpp}}.

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_a146eb84093b492d9674b6eaed24eec47}\label{classSourceSinkData_a146eb84093b492d9674b6eaed24eec47} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!PerformRegressionVsOMAndSize@{PerformRegressionVsOMAndSize}}
\index{PerformRegressionVsOMAndSize@{PerformRegressionVsOMAndSize}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{PerformRegressionVsOMAndSize()}{PerformRegressionVsOMAndSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Perform\+Regression\+Vs\+OMAnd\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const string \&}]{om,  }\item[{const string \&}]{particle\+\_\+size,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{multiplelinearregression_8h_a126d68f6f19dcf3ad6b16e179766a91f}{regression\+\_\+form}}}]{form,  }\item[{const double \&}]{p\+\_\+value\+\_\+threshold = {\ttfamily 0.05} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs multiple linear regression of elements vs OM and particle size. 

Computes regression models for all sample groups to quantify how elemental concentrations vary with organic matter (OM) content and particle size. These models are used to correct elemental profiles for OM/size variations.

Regression forms\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Linear\+: C\+\_\+corrected = C + β₁(OM\+\_\+ref -\/ OM) + β₂(Size\+\_\+ref -\/ Size)
\item Multiplicative\+: C\+\_\+corrected = C × (OM\+\_\+ref/\+OM)\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}β₁ × (Size\+\_\+ref/\+Size)\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}β₂
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em om} & Name of the organic matter constituent (e.\+g., "{}\+OC"{}, "{}\+OM"{}) \\
\hline
{\em particle\+\_\+size} & Name of the particle size constituent (e.\+g., "{}\+D50"{}, "{}\+PM2.\+5"{}) \\
\hline
{\em form} & Regression form (linear or multiplicative) \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+value\+\_\+threshold} & Significance threshold for including predictors (default\+: 0.\+05)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if regressions were computed successfully
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Stores OM and size constituent names for later correction 

Regressions are computed for all groups (sources and target) 

Predictors with p \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} threshold are excluded from the model
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{classSourceSinkData_a594ab5813abb8fa2cad92f0e98bbd304}{Get\+MLRResults()} to retrieve regression results 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8cpp_source_l02781}{2781}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8cpp_source}{sourcesinkdata.\+cpp}}.

Referenced by \mbox{\hyperlink{conductor_8cpp_source_l00561}{Conductor\+::\+Execute\+MLR()}}.

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_a89f22f243adbc94da12f4c4b0a46e96d}\label{classSourceSinkData_a89f22f243adbc94da12f4c4b0a46e96d} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!PopulateConstituentOrders@{PopulateConstituentOrders}}
\index{PopulateConstituentOrders@{PopulateConstituentOrders}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{PopulateConstituentOrders()}{PopulateConstituentOrders()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Populate\+Constituent\+Orders (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Populates all element ordering vectors used throughout CMB analysis. 

Scans the element information map and organizes elements into separate ordering vectors based on their roles. These vectors define the order in which elements appear in matrices, parameter vectors, and observations.

Populated Vectors\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item constituent\+\_\+order\+\_\+\+: All species in the dataset
\item element\+\_\+order\+\_\+\+: Chemical elements flagged for analysis
\item isotope\+\_\+order\+\_\+\+: Isotopes flagged for analysis
\item size\+\_\+om\+\_\+order\+\_\+\+: Particle size and organic carbon parameters
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Must be called before \doxylink{classSourceSinkData_a08a9298df90991f6735134ae8d6a0955}{Initialize\+Parameters\+And\+Observations()} 
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!ResidualJacobian\_arma@{ResidualJacobian\_arma}}
\index{ResidualJacobian\_arma@{ResidualJacobian\_arma}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ResidualJacobian\_arma()}{ResidualJacobian\_arma()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily CMatrix\+\_\+arma Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Residual\+Jacobian\+\_\+arma (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Calculates the Jacobian matrix of residuals with respect to contributions (Armadillo) 

Computes the numerical derivative of the residual vector with respect to the first (n-\/1) source contributions using finite differences.

The Jacobian matrix J has dimensions \mbox{[}(n-\/1) sources × (elements + isotopes)\mbox{]}, where J\mbox{[}i,j\mbox{]} = ∂residual\+\_\+j / ∂contribution\+\_\+i

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
CMatrix\+\_\+arma Jacobian matrix in Armadillo format
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Uses adaptive epsilon based on distance from contribution = 0.\+5 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily CMatrix Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Residual\+Jacobian\+\_\+softmax (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Calculates the Jacobian using softmax parameterization of contributions. 

Computes the numerical derivative of residuals with respect to unconstrained softmax parameters. Includes all n sources since softmax transformation ensures contributions sum to 1 automatically.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
CMatrix Jacobian matrix (n sources × m observations)
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Uses sign-\/dependent epsilon for better numerical behavior 
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ResidualVector()}{ResidualVector()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily CVector Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Residual\+Vector (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Calculates the combined residual vector for elemental and isotopic predictions. 

Computes residuals between predicted and observed values for both elemental concentrations (in log-\/space) and isotopic delta values (in linear space).

Combined residual vector structure\+: \mbox{[}log(C\+\_\+pred/\+C\+\_\+obs) for each element, δ\+\_\+pred -\/ δ\+\_\+obs for each isotope\mbox{]}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
CVector of combined residuals
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Returns vector with non-\/finite values if predictions are invalid 
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SetParameterValue()}{SetParameterValue()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Set\+Parameter\+Value (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{index,  }\item[{double}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets a parameter value and updates corresponding model components. 

Updates a parameter in the parameter vector and synchronizes the change with the appropriate model component (contributions, distribution parameters, or error terms). The parameter vector layout depends on the estimation mode.

\doxylink{classParameter}{Parameter} Vector Layout (full mode\+: elemental\+\_\+profile\+\_\+and\+\_\+contribution)\+: \mbox{[}0 to n-\/2\mbox{]}\+: \doxylink{classContribution}{Contribution} parameters (n-\/1 sources) \mbox{[}n-\/1 to end of element μ\mbox{]}\+: Element μ parameters \mbox{[}element μ to end of isotope μ\mbox{]}\+: Isotope μ parameters \mbox{[}isotope μ to end of element σ\mbox{]}\+: Element σ parameters \mbox{[}element σ to end of isotope σ\mbox{]}\+: Isotope σ parameters \mbox{[}end-\/1\mbox{]}\+: Error std dev for elements \mbox{[}end\mbox{]}\+: Error std dev for isotopes


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em index} & \doxylink{classParameter}{Parameter} index in the parameters\+\_\+ vector \\
\hline
{\em value} & New parameter value \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if parameter was successfully updated, false if index is invalid
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Automatically updates last contribution to maintain sum constraint

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SolveLevenberg\_Marquardt()}{SolveLevenberg\_Marquardt()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Solve\+Levenberg\+\_\+\+Marquardt (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8h_a11d668d69b6bca08871d520d0315e9e1}{transformation}}}]{trans = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8h_a11d668d69b6bca08871d520d0315e9e1a9a932b3cb396238423eb2f33ec17d6aa}{transformation\+::linear}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Solves for optimal source contributions using the Levenberg-\/\+Marquardt algorithm. 

Iteratively optimizes source contributions to minimize the residual between predicted and observed elemental/isotopic compositions. The algorithm adaptively adjusts the damping parameter based on convergence behavior.

Convergence criteria (any of)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Residual norm \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} tolerance (1e-\/10)
\item \doxylink{classParameter}{Parameter} change norm \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} tolerance (1e-\/10)
\item Maximum iterations reached (1000)
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em trans} & Parameterization method\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{sourcesinkdata_8h_a11d668d69b6bca08871d520d0315e9e1a9a932b3cb396238423eb2f33ec17d6aa}{transformation\+::linear}\+: Direct contribution values with constraint Σc\+\_\+i = 1
\item \doxylink{sourcesinkdata_8h_a11d668d69b6bca08871d520d0315e9e1ace2f1fbd249d24aabc07ac4488ab5b8c}{transformation\+::softmax}\+: Unconstrained parameters transformed via softmax
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
bool Currently always returns false (legacy)
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Updates internal state with optimized contributions 

Progress displayed in rtw\+\_\+ if set 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classCMBVector}{CMBVector}} $>$ Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Stepwise\+Discriminant\+Function\+Analysis (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const string \&}]{source1,  }\item[{const string \&}]{source2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs stepwise discriminant analysis between two specific sources. 

Iteratively selects elements that best discriminate between two source groups using a forward selection procedure. At each step, adds the element that most improves group separation (lowest p-\/value).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em source1} & Name of first source group \\
\hline
{\em source2} & Name of second source group\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Elements ordered by discriminating power (best first) 

Progress updates sent to rtw\+\_\+ if available 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_a498d4ebf48c3a462b5107fca33d81564}\label{classSourceSinkData_a498d4ebf48c3a462b5107fca33d81564} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!t\_TestPValue@{t\_TestPValue}}
\index{t\_TestPValue@{t\_TestPValue}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{t\_TestPValue()}{t\_TestPValue()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classElemental__Profile}{Elemental\+\_\+\+Profile}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::t\+\_\+\+Test\+PValue (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const string \&}]{source1,  }\item[{const string \&}]{source2,  }\item[{bool}]{use\+\_\+log }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes t-\/test p-\/values for element-\/wise differences between two sources. 

Performs independent two-\/sample t-\/tests for each element to assess whether concentrations differ significantly between two source groups. Lower p-\/values indicate stronger evidence that the sources differ for that element.

T-\/statistic\+: t = (μ₁ -\/ μ₂) / √(σ₁²/n₁ + σ₂²/n₂)


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em source1} & Name of first source group \\
\hline
{\em source2} & Name of second source group \\
\hline
{\em use\+\_\+log} & If true, perform test on log-\/transformed concentrations; if false, use linear-\/space concentrations\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classElemental__Profile}{Elemental\+\_\+\+Profile} containing two-\/tailed p-\/values for each element
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
P-\/values are two-\/tailed (tests for any difference, not directional) 

Lower p-\/values indicate better source differentiation 

Log-\/space testing appropriate for log-\/normally distributed data
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_aac25198517d6efee29b18a8b3d641636}\label{classSourceSinkData_aac25198517d6efee29b18a8b3d641636} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!TotalScatterMatrix@{TotalScatterMatrix}}
\index{TotalScatterMatrix@{TotalScatterMatrix}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{TotalScatterMatrix()}{TotalScatterMatrix()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily CMatrix Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Total\+Scatter\+Matrix (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Computes total scatter matrix. 

Calculates the overall covariance matrix treating all source samples as a single population. Represents total variability.

Formula\+: S\+\_\+T = Σ Σ\mbox{[}(x\+\_\+ij -\/ μ\+\_\+overall)(x\+\_\+ij -\/ μ\+\_\+overall)ᵀ\mbox{]} / N

Relationship\+: S\+\_\+T = S\+\_\+W + S\+\_\+B

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Total scatter matrix (num\+\_\+elements × num\+\_\+elements)
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Target group excluded 
\end{DoxyNote}


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8cpp_source_l04512}{4512}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{sourcesinkdata_8cpp_source}{sourcesinkdata.\+cpp}}.

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_a7ed4c3053a2afaa56bd01f93da5c0a8f}\label{classSourceSinkData_a7ed4c3053a2afaa56bd01f93da5c0a8f} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!VerifySource@{VerifySource}}
\index{VerifySource@{VerifySource}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{VerifySource()}{VerifySource()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classCMBTimeSeriesSet}{CMBTime\+Series\+Set}} Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Verify\+Source (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const string \&}]{source\+\_\+group,  }\item[{bool}]{use\+\_\+softmax,  }\item[{bool}]{apply\+\_\+om\+\_\+size\+\_\+correction }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs leave-\/one-\/out validation on a source group. 

Tests source apportionment accuracy by iteratively treating each sample from a source group as an unknown target, solving the CMB model, and comparing estimated contributions against the known true source.

Ideal result\+: Sample shows \texorpdfstring{$\sim$}{\string~}100\% contribution from its true source


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em source\+\_\+group} & Name of source group to validate \\
\hline
{\em use\+\_\+softmax} & If true, use softmax transformation for contributions \\
\hline
{\em apply\+\_\+om\+\_\+size\+\_\+correction} & If true, apply OM and size corrections\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{classCMBTimeSeriesSet}{CMBTime\+Series\+Set} containing contribution estimates for each sample
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Samples with negative values after correction are skipped 

Progress updates sent to rtw\+\_\+ if available 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{classSourceSinkData_a4c5fa40683b34fb16227aaeb2f374b41}\label{classSourceSinkData_a4c5fa40683b34fb16227aaeb2f374b41} 
\index{SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}!WilksLambda@{WilksLambda}}
\index{WilksLambda@{WilksLambda}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{WilksLambda()}{WilksLambda()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily double Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Wilks\+Lambda (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Computes Wilks\textquotesingle{} Lambda statistic for multivariate group separation. 

Calculates Wilks\textquotesingle{} Lambda, a multivariate test statistic measuring the ratio of within-\/group to total variance.

Formula\+: Λ = \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\+S\+\_\+\+W\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} / \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\+S\+\_\+\+T\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} = \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\+S\+\_\+\+W\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} / \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\+S\+\_\+W + S\+\_\+\+B\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}

Interpretation\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Λ = 1\+: No group separation
\item Λ → 0\+: Perfect separation
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Wilks\textquotesingle{} Lambda statistic (0 to 1)
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Uses absolute values of determinants for numerical stability 
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{WithinGroupCovarianceMatrix@{WithinGroupCovarianceMatrix}!SourceSinkData@{SourceSinkData}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{WithinGroupCovarianceMatrix()}{WithinGroupCovarianceMatrix()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily CMatrix Source\+Sink\+Data\+::\+Within\+Group\+Covariance\+Matrix (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Computes pooled within-\/group covariance matrix. 

Calculates the weighted average of covariance matrices within each source group. Represents the "{}error"{} or within-\/group scatter in discriminant analysis.

Formula\+: S\+\_\+W = Σ\mbox{[}(n\+\_\+i -\/ 1) × Σ\+\_\+i\mbox{]} / Σ(n\+\_\+i -\/ 1)

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Within-\/group covariance matrix (num\+\_\+elements × num\+\_\+elements)
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Target group excluded 

Weighted by degrees of freedom (n\+\_\+i -\/ 1) 
\end{DoxyNote}
